    FROM [Patients] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[UserId] = @__userId_0
) AS [p0]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Dosage], [m].[DrugId], [m].[EndDate], [m].[FrequencyPerWeek], [m].[InsertedAt], [m].[ModifiedAt], [m].[PatientId], [m].[StartDate], [d].[Id] AS [Id0], [d].[Company], [d].[InsertedAt] AS [InsertedAt0], [d].[ModifiedAt] AS [ModifiedAt0], [d].[Name], [d].[PackageSize]

) AS [s] ON [p0].[Id] = [s].[PatientId]
